Current Commentary

On the Character of Politicians 18

Amidst the clamorous calls and urgent requests, Jiang and Wang, after their meeting in Hangzhou, entered Beijing together. The central government began to show some vitality, and the political situation began to show some signs of change. However, just as Jiang and Wang arrived, Premier Sun Ke suddenly resigned. The bizarre changes and twists of the political situation truly leave people unable to comprehend or grasp.

Tracing back to the split between Ningbo and Yue last year, the disturbances and disputes, and the outbreak of the September 18th Incident, the stimuli from foreign aggression, and the envoys of peace, were constantly on the road, negotiating painstakingly. The Yue faction insisted on Jiang's resignation as a prerequisite. It was as if "If this person does not leave, the disaster will not end." Finally, Mr. Jiang retired, and the political situation took a sharp turn for the worse. A new government was born with difficulty, but the key figures of the party and the state were all ill for a time. Hu was ill in Yue, Wang was ill in Shanghai, and Jiang was leisurely enjoying himself on Miaogao Terrace, enjoying his solitude. The central government was empty, and there was no one in charge. Everything was scattered like sand, and nothing could be done. Therefore, the call to urge the three leaders to enter Beijing arose in response to the times. The envoys urging them to come were constantly on the road. Even Mr. Sun himself went to Hangzhou to urge Jiang to enter Beijing. At that time, the situation was as if "If this person does not come out, what will happen to the people?" Now Wang and Jiang have already entered Beijing and are already in power. However, Mr. Sun, as the Premier of the responsible cabinet, suddenly came to Shanghai in a hurry and resigned in a hurry. What followed was the retention and urging. In the past month, the diplomatic situation has become increasingly urgent, while the government authorities are busy avoiding responsibility and urging each other to take office. Sometimes they object, sometimes they welcome, sometimes they are active, sometimes they are discouraged. With joys and sorrows, separations and reunions, and all kinds of changes, we truly do not know whether the government authorities are playing a game of hide-and-seek, or suffering from the capricious disease of children, or whether the government authorities are all drunkards, so that they help each other to the east, but then they fall to the west. In this situation, we truly cannot distinguish right from wrong, and we cannot laugh or cry. Since the September 18th Incident, the leaders of the party and the state have been proclaiming to the people every day that they will seek peace, unity, and sincere solidarity to overcome national difficulties together. However, in reality, they come and go, each with their own hidden agendas, as incompatible as ice and coal. Now the diplomatic situation is becoming increasingly dangerous. Looking around the world, everyone is watching each other, silent. In this situation, if the authorities still cannot gather the strength of the whole country and risk their lives to seek survival, but instead use diplomatic issues as a tool for political struggle and disregard the national crisis, what is their mentality? We truly cannot find an answer even after thinking about it a hundred times.

We believe that the national situation today has reached an extremely serious level, on the verge of collapse, with survival at stake. The country belongs to all the people of the country, and it is absolutely not allowed for a small number of people to sit idly by and make mistakes. It is especially not allowed for a small number of people to be obsessed with the pursuit of power and accelerate its demise. The people of the country are enduring death and waiting for orders. Now is the final moment. If the government does not want to inevitably cause the country to perish and the race to be destroyed, then it should temporarily abandon selfish desires and strive for unity, and shift the spirit of vying for power to saving the country and resisting foreign aggression. If it cannot, then it should return the political power to our people, giving the people the opportunity to save the country. We dare to solemnly declare that from now on, the people of the country will no longer allow national affairs to be the exclusive property of a small number of people. Politicians should have the character of statesmen. If they continue to treat national affairs as a child's play, they will not only be unable to establish a country, but also unable to establish themselves. All these actions, if thought about in the quiet of the night, should also be disturbing. Why are they still ignorant and unaware?

Opening on February 11th

Central Standing Committee

Letter of Retention for Sun Ke 22

(Nanjing) The Central Standing Committee sent a letter of retention to Sun Ke. We unanimously decided to retain you and immediately telegraphed back to request you to withdraw your resignation. We hope you will understand. We have now publicly appointed Ju Juesheng, Zhang Puquan, and Zhang Jingjiang to go to Shanghai to explain everything in detail. At this time of serious national crisis, the central government cannot be without someone in charge for even a day. We hope that you will immediately return to Beijing with the three comrades to preside over government affairs, and never be discouraged. The future of the Party and the country depends on this. We sincerely implore you to consider this carefully and wish you Party peace." (Special Dispatch of the 26th)

(Nanjing) The Central Standing Committee telegraphed Sun Ke, President of the Executive Yuan, on the 25th, hoping that he would withdraw his resignation and come to Beijing soon. The original telegram read: "Comrade Sun Zhesheng: We have received your telegram. The national crisis is urgent, and the central administration has just been organized and put in order. It must not be changed suddenly to increase the difficulty of diplomacy and shake the foundation of the Party and the country. Comrades have high expectations and are especially reliant on you. We hope that you will uphold your original intention of taking responsibility and overcome difficulties, withdraw your resignation, and come to Beijing soon. We are eagerly awaiting." (Special Dispatch of the 26th)

Zhou Fo Hai Requests Levy of Cigarette Surtax

The remainder will be paid in installments, and the Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office will be ordered to allocate the arrears of 165,000 yuan for one and a half months to Central University; (2) The funds for national colleges and universities for January should be ordered to be issued within this month; (3) The arrears of primary and secondary schools in Hubei and Anhui provinces should be subsidized by the central government; (4) The requests of national colleges and universities and middle schools in Hubei and Anhui for fixed funds for the expenses of each school should be accepted, and Liu Ruiheng, Duan Xipeng, Jia Shiyi, and Zheng Hongnian will be designated to draft measures for submission and approval. Zheng will convene a meeting at the Executive Yuan on the 27th to discuss the measures. (Special Dispatch of the 26th)

(Special Dispatch of the 26th)

(Nanjing) Zhou Fohai, Director of the Jiangsu Education Department, telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education, advocating that an additional surtax be levied on the special cigarette tax in Jiangsu Province to fund Central University to make up for the shortfall. [Notice from the Peiping Public Security Bureau to Various Newspapers]

Be Careful When Reporting News About the Japanese Emperor 25

Japanese Acting Envoy Yano Meets with Zhang Xueliang

Demanding the Closure of the Peking Leader Newspaper

(Peiping) The Public Security Bureau notified various newspapers today, stating that the Peking Morning Post had previously been suspended for one day because it contained information involving the Japanese Imperial Family. Now, the Peking Leader newspaper has also published the same information. Negotiations are currently underway. As the diplomatic situation is tense, all matters relating to the Japanese Imperial Family and the Japanese military must be reported with caution in the future, and nothing should be given to the enemy to exploit. (Special Dispatch of the 26th)

(Peiping) Reuters learned today that Japanese Acting Envoy Yano met with Zhang Xueliang on Saturday and Sunday, stating that the English-language Peking Leader's editorial on Korean affairs insulted Japan and demanded the permanent closure of the newspaper, the arrest of the author of the article, Mr. Li, and an apology to Japan. Mediation on this matter has been ineffective for days. Yano stated that this matter is in the hands of the Japanese Foreign Ministry in Tokyo, and he is now acting in accordance with instructions. According to the latest reports, the Peking Leader is the only English-language daily newspaper in Peiping in the past two years. A spokesman for the Japanese Embassy stated this afternoon that the Peking Leader has been criticizing Japan in recent months, and the Japanese have been patiently enduring it. The cause of this incident was the Morning Post's earlier publication of a declaration from the Korean Independence Federation, which contained many insulting remarks against Japan. After negotiations with the Chinese authorities, a satisfactory outcome was obtained. Unexpectedly, the next day, the Leader translated and published the declaration, and although disrespectful words were deleted, the Japanese still regarded it as an insult. The next day, the newspaper published an editorial on Korean affairs, so the Japanese party requested Zhang Xueliang to deal with it in a severe manner. It is heard that the reporter of the newspaper, Mr. Li, is now willing to leave Peiping temporarily, hoping that the matter can be resolved. According to semi-official sources, Zhang Xueliang has not yet acknowledged the Japanese demands. (Reuters Dispatch of the 26th)

Important Foreign Telegrams

Shanghai Incident Situation Dire 66

The Japanese Government Resolves to Adopt Emergency Measures

To Deal with China's Passive National Salvation Movement

Two Japanese Military Aircraft Arrive in Shanghai Today

Kobe Buddhist Monk Vows to Avenge His Teacher and Brother

National News Agency, Tokyo, 26th: According to the Foreign Ministry today, Foreign Minister Yoshizawa will send a practical instruction regarding the Shanghai incident to Murai, the Japanese Consul General in Shanghai. It is reported that the Japanese authorities, due to Shanghai Mayor Wu's failure to reply to Murai, have decided to protect Japanese residents in Shanghai with strict and effective plans. It is also reported that after receiving the instruction, Murai will consult with Rear Admiral Shiozawa and others to deal with the anti-Japanese national salvation associations with emergency measures. Furthermore, Tokyo naval authorities have also decided that if the Chinese authorities do not provide a satisfactory answer to Japan's demands, they will take action against anti-Japanese elements in Shanghai. Therefore, the Shanghai situation may undergo drastic changes in the next 48 hours.

National News Agency, Tokyo, 26th: Japanese Ambassador to China Shigemitsu denied that he will arrive in Shanghai tomorrow and that the final solution to the Sino-Japanese dispute will be determined after his arrival in Shanghai. Shigemitsu is scheduled to depart on the Nagasaki Maru on Thursday, and his arrival in Shanghai will be on Sunday. The Shanghai negotiation is still being handled by Japanese Consul General Murai, acting on instructions from the Japanese Foreign Ministry, in conjunction with Rear Admiral Shiozawa, commander of the Japanese fleet. Shiozawa is constantly communicating with the Tokyo Naval Ministry. The Cabinet again discussed the Shanghai incident yesterday. Because Naval Minister Osumi is ill in bed, the Vice Minister reported on the situation in Shanghai. It is reported that the Cabinet resolved to exert its determination to protect Japanese residents in Shanghai.

United Press, Tokyo, 26th: The Cabinet met at 11:00 AM today. Naval Minister Osumi explained the situation in Shanghai in detail. As a result of the exchange of opinions, it was unanimously agreed that if decisive measures are not taken at this time, it will be difficult to ensure the safety of the lives and property of Japanese residents. Therefore, it was decided to make every effort to advance according to the established policy.

Reuters, Tokyo, 26th: Responsible sources today stated that Japan is determined to resolve China's organized anti-Japanese movement. Authorities commented on the Shanghai situation, saying that Japan's actions depend entirely on China's actions, but will not disturb the Public Concession. Although the government acknowledges the seriousness of the overall situation, it still hopes that the incident will not escalate, as the new Nanjing government is now adopting a rational attitude towards Japan and is apparently prepared to curb the illegal activities of anti-Japanese groups.

National News Agency, Nagasaki, 26th: Sasebo has already dispatched three military aircraft, transported to Shanghai by the Shanghai Maru for the use of the Marines, which can arrive tomorrow afternoon.

Reuters, Tokyo, 26th: Several warships were ordered to sail to China today, presumably to Shanghai, but details are kept secret. It is believed that there are a cruiser and twelve destroyers, which have been preparing for departure in Sasebo since Friday.

Dentsu, Nagasaki, 26th: Kiyomizu Keishu, the chief priest of Myohoji Temple in Kobe, departed from Nagasaki for Shanghai on the Shanghai Maru today. Kiyomizu and the late Amazaki Keisho, who was killed in Shanghai, were teacher and brother. According to Kiyomizu, he and Keisho went to India with Nissho last year, and later struggled for the sect in China. Unexpectedly, Keisho sacrificed himself this time. After I arrive in Shanghai, I will consult with the military and will not return without avenging Keisho's death.

Britain and the United States to Take Joint Action on the Shanghai Situation 67

Intend to Lodge a Serious Protest with Japan

U.S. Consul General Ordered to Act at His Discretion

National News Agency, Washington, 25th: Although the State Department has not issued any statement regarding the tense situation in Shanghai, government officials have expressed that they are very concerned about any independent actions by Japanese troops in the Shanghai Public Concession. U.S. Consul General in Shanghai Cunningham is in close contact with the State Department. It is reported that the State Department has given Cunningham the authority to act at his discretion and has also given this authority to Admiral Tana, commander of the U.S. Asiatic Fleet, who can move his ships at will without first consulting the Navy Department.

Reuters, New York, 26th: The New York Times this morning published a special dispatch from Washington, stating that Washington has the impression that the United States is considering taking forceful action, either jointly with Britain or independently, regarding the landing of Japanese Marines in Shanghai. The New York Tribune's Washington special dispatch stated that there are various signs that the United States will lodge a forceful protest against Japanese actions in the Public Concession. A government spokesman has subtly warned that the actions of the Japanese in the Concession will be indefensible and unforgivable.

Reuters, London, 26th: The Liberal Party's news bulletin commented on the possibility of Japanese troops occupying Shanghai, saying that Japan is using the excuse that the Chinese government cannot maintain law and order, but the dominance of the Japanese military authorities over their own government is becoming increasingly tight and may lead to surprising results that are difficult to limit. The extreme intimidation plan damages the dignity of the Chinese government and only worsens the situation.

Soviet Russia and Poland Sign Non-Aggression Pact 68

Reuters, Moscow, 26th: The Soviet Russian government intends to conclude non-aggression pacts with its neighboring countries. It recently concluded such a pact with Finland, and now it has concluded such a pact with Poland. Diplomats from both countries gathered here today.

National News Agency, Moscow, 25th: The non-aggression pact signed between Soviet Russia and Poland was signed here today and will take effect soon. Moscow still hopes to conclude a similar treaty with Japan.

Japan Borrows Money from France 69

Totaling 800 Million Francs

Used to Pay for the Purchase of Military Equipment

National News Agency, Berlin, 25th: According to a report from Paris, a French banking consortium, led by the Bank of France, recently agreed to lend 800 million francs to Japan. The majority of this loan will be used to pay for military equipment purchased by Japan in France. Various industries in France are experiencing a recession, and many workers are being laid off. Only the arms industry is particularly prosperous. In recent months, a well-known arms factory has even added 55,000 workers.

French Air Ministry Adds Sky Warfare Weapon 70

Planning Four New Squadrons of Bomber Aircraft

Capable of Carrying Five Heavy Artillery Pieces 10,000 Feet into the Air

National News Agency, Paris, 25th: According to reports, the French Air Ministry has ordered four new squadrons of bomber aircraft from French aircraft factories. Each squadron can carry one ton of bombs. In addition to ten machine gunners, it can also carry more than 20 people to operate five heavy artillery pieces installed on the wings and tail, capable of rising to 12,000 feet. The average speed per hour can reach 200 miles. This military weapon is known as the "Sky Tank."

Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Goes to Geneva 71

To Attend the Disarmament Conference

National News Agency, Moscow, 26th: Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov, along with his staff, left for Geneva today to participate in the World Disarmament Conference, which will open on February 2nd. The Soviet Russian delegation will push for the greatest possible disarmament in Geneva. Soviet Russia continues to pursue a policy of peace and advocates for the equitable restriction of all military equipment in accordance with straightforward treaties.

National News Agency, London, 26th: British experts today claimed that the upcoming Disarmament Conference may discuss the abolition of aircraft carriers because of their exorbitant cost. The United States had long considered it too expensive, as the two warships of this type built by the United States cost 100 million US dollars. Moreover, since aircraft can now take off and land from battleships, submarines, etc., aircraft carriers are now considered redundant. Currently, Britain, the United States, and Japan each have two of these ships, while France and Italy each have one.

Spanish General Strike Not Realized 72

Barcelona Communists Still Active

Reuters, Madrid, 26th: The general strike announced on the 25th was not realized. According to news today, the cities are still quiet, with only a few demonstrations occurring. Madrid is operating as usual. However, extremist elements are holding meetings. Several people were arrested by the authorities for announcing the general strike today. The Communist Party in Barcelona, previously controlled by the police, attempted to act recklessly, but was suppressed by government troops. Yesterday, a group of communists stormed into the university, attempting to intimidate the students, viewing the students as enemies. The students did not show weakness. The communists were forced to flee into trams and were eventually arrested by the police. Three or four people were arrested. However, the general strike in Seville is quite effective. Trams and streetcars have stopped running, but military aircraft are flying incessantly in the sky. Machine guns have been placed at key points in the city. Due to effective prevention, there has been no major unrest.

Reuters, Barcelona, 26th: It is reported that a communist government has been established in Alcora. Municipal funds, railways, and explosive depots have been confiscated. Troops have been dispatched here today to suppress them. Alcora is a small province with approximately 3,160 residents.

Cheng Yun Talks About Bin County Provincial Government Situation 75

The Dissolution of the Provincial Government Requires a Central Government Order

I am Not Afraid of Airplanes and Artillery Even if it Costs Me My Life

A correspondent from Harbin visited Cheng Yun, Chairman of the Jilin Provisional Provincial Government in Bin County, and had the following conversation: (Q) Chairman, you have taken on a difficult task this time in organizing the provincial government. Can you tell us the story of the provincial government moving to Bin County? (A) After the Japanese army invaded Liaoning and Jilin, when the provincial government held a committee meeting, I strongly advocated resistance. Unfortunately, we lacked the strength to do so. After the Japanese army entered the city, they forced me to serve as the president of the High Court. I did not want to be a puppet official under Japanese rule, so I disguised myself and escaped. Because the cost of living in Beiping was low, I initially planned to move to Beiping and live a civilian life. When the train arrived in Jinzhou, I received a telegram from Beiping ordering me to return to Harbin to organize the government. Considering the importance of the matter, I detoured through the Taoang Railway to Harbin. Because of various inconveniences in Harbin, I submitted a report to the National Government, which approved the relocation of the Jilin Provincial Government to Bin County. (Q) Have there been any difficulties since the establishment of the provincial government? (A) There is nothing easy in China now. If we are afraid of difficulties, there is nothing we can do. There were no major difficulties in organizing the provincial government this time. In fact, even if there were difficulties, as a modern Chinese, we should not talk about difficulties. (Q) How many provincial committee members are currently in Bin County? (A) Myself, Director Xu of the Finance Department, and Secretary-General 　 are the three. (Q) Why haven't the other provincial committee members come? (A) Rong Hou and Zhang Qihuai, two provincial committee members, could not come due to illness. Wang Zhiyou and Zhong Yu, two provincial committee members, were too busy with official duties in Harbin and could not come either. (Q) Who is responsible for the military of each brigade under the jurisdiction of the provincial government? (A) Li Ziluo, the Training Supervisor and current Deputy Commander, is fully responsible for military affairs. However, the provincial government is responsible for raising military pay. (Q) Is it true that there are rumors that Wang Zhiyou and others have an unclear attitude? (A) Wang and others are all my old friends of many years, and their character is very noble. There is absolutely no possibility of an unclear attitude. (Q) What is the chairman's opinion on the Jilin side requesting the dissolution of the provincial government? (A) I have no preconceived notions about the existence or non-existence of the provincial government. However, I came here to organize the provincial government under the explicit order of the Central Government and the entrustment of Deputy Commander (Zhang Zuoxiang). Now I can only obey the instructions of the Central Government and the Deputy Commander. As for myself, I have no preconceived notions. (Q) If the Bin Provincial Government is not abolished, the people will inevitably suffer. (A) The people will inevitably suffer. However, if the situation deteriorates, I am afraid the Chinese people will have no happiness to speak of. (Q) It is heard that after the provincial government was bombed, many personnel scattered, and it is also heard that the provincial government plans to move to Yilan. Is this true? (A) The personnel who have come here to work are mostly patriots who are not afraid of difficulties, and their numbers are increasing day by day, which shows that the hearts of the people have not yet died. As for the claim of moving to Yilan, the provincial government has absolutely no intention of doing so. (Q) Were you frightened by the Japanese planes dropping bombs? (A) I came here to take risks and have already put life and death out of my mind. I have nothing else, and I am not afraid of artillery and airplanes at all. (Q) What is the situation of the war in the front lines of Wuchang and Yushu? (A) This time, the infighting among compatriots is the most shameful thing. However, because Yu Xizhou led his troops to force an invasion, we had no choice but to send Commander Feng to Wuchang and other places for self-defense, not to seek war. (Q) What is the attitude of the original Jilin brigades? (A) The brigade commanders of Jilin are all old comrades of the Deputy Commander for many years and are extremely reliable. Their attitude can be seen from the troop movements this time. Other matters are related to military secrets, so it is not convenient to disclose them. Finally, Cheng said that he came here purely to maintain national sovereignty and uphold the rule of law and would never yield until death. Please do not lightly believe various anti-propaganda from the outside world. We also hope that the public opinion circle will uphold justice and promote integrity, so that the hearts of the people will not die and the national destiny can be extended. (January 18)

Zhang Zuoxiang Resigns and Comes to Tianjin 76

A Tianjin correspondent reports that Jilin Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Zuoxiang, feeling ashamed and pained by the loss of the Northeast, recently wrote to Zhang Xueliang, earnestly requesting him to forward his resignation from all concurrent positions to the Central Government and to punish him for losing national territory. Zhang Xueliang telegraphed the Central Government. It is unknown whether his request will be approved, but his determination to leave is very firm. Therefore, he resolutely left Beiping with his family last night and came to Tianjin. His adjutant Song Changyan accompanied him. Other subordinates all came to notify the train, which arrived at the Tianjin station at 12:00 midnight. Other than Qian Mingyu, his Tianjin advisor, who came to the station to take care of him, no one else came to greet him, probably because the local authorities were unaware of his arrival.

According to Zhang, he told the reporter that the Shenyang Incident cut off his return route. For several months, he has relied entirely on telegrams to maintain the morale of the Jilin defense, with two or thirty telegrams a day covering a distance of more than two thousand miles. His 25th Brigade, the core of the Jilin army, stationed in Yushu, was most feared by the Japanese army. Yushu had 8,000 militiamen who were willing to assist the 25th Brigade in resisting the enemy. Initially, because the overall plan was undecided and it was difficult to advance or retreat, they did not dare to act rashly. Until January 9th, Xi Qia, willing to be a slave, under the cover of more than ten Japanese planes, led his bandit army of about three brigades and a mixed Japanese army of about one brigade to attack Yushu fiercely. Our 25th Brigade and 8,000 militiamen joined together to meet them. They fought bloodily day and night, killing countless enemies. However, man has his limits. We had no reinforcements. Each soldier had only 200 rounds of ammunition, and the equipment was faulty. It was obvious that the final victory would belong to the elite enemy, even a three-year-old child could know this. As expected, by January 18, the defeat of our army was complete. However, if it were not for the treachery of the militiamen, the entire army would not have been annihilated. Now Xi Qia's bandit soldiers have mixed with the militiamen. I could have mobilized the army of the Chinese Eastern Railway under my command to fight these people to the death, but I fear that the result would be the same whether we fight or not, and fighting would only increase the devastation of the region and the burden on our homeland. I also fear that it would trigger Sino-Russian negotiations, so I am willing to endure humiliation and pain and await the Central Government's decision on the overall plan before determining the next steps. However, I can endure, but the people of the Northeast can no longer endure. For the past ten days, people's organizations as far as two thousand miles away have sent telegrams questioning the plan. I have to ask Zhang, and Zhang has to obey the Central Government. Since the Shenyang Incident, the Central Government has still had no practical plan, going back and forth without being able to do anything. I have failed to defend the territory and deserve to be punished. Continuing like this will only increase my sins. Therefore, I have decided to resign and request punishment. Once a plan for recovery is in place, I will go east with a guilty body to kill the enemy and hopefully atone for my past mistakes. (January 24)

Kidnapping of Three People in Dale Village, Huzhou. In the eastern part of Dale Village, about three miles from Yigao in the northern part of this city, lives Li Boying, a resident with some assets. He was targeted by bandits. On the afternoon of the 22nd of this month, around 6:00 PM, a dozen bandits, armed with wooden-cased guns and pistols, stormed in through the side door. At the time, Boying was having dinner and managed to hide under a worker's bed, avoiding being kidnapped. The bandits then kidnapped Li's younger brother, Bao, and nephew, Lu Kangru, and went to the home of a Mr. Shen in the same village, stealing over fifty silver dollars and kidnapping Shen's young son, speeding away westward by boat. 80

Xiaoshan: Investigation of Cooperative Society Dispute. Xiaoshan is the pioneering county for cooperative ventures in Zhejiang Province, and they have been relatively successful. However, a dispute arose between the Linpu Puliu Cooperative Society and the Tianle Cooperative Society over goods. The case is in litigation, but the court has not yet made a decision. Suddenly, a brawl occurred between the Tianle Township Cooperative Society and the Puliu Cooperative Society, making the dispute even more difficult to resolve. Fearing that this continued conflict would hinder the future promotion of cooperative societies and their benefits, the Construction Department dispatched a special investigator to conduct a thorough investigation, detailed inspection, and division of areas to prevent encroachment and further incidents. 81

Provincial Department Establishes Method for Collecting Land Tax. The Xiaoshan County Government yesterday received instructions from the Provincial Finance Department stating that the land, fields, and swamps in various counties of Zhejiang Province should have their land tax collected at the original rate of one dollar and eighty cents per tael of silver and three dollars and thirty cents per shi (unit of dry measure) of rice. The first installment will include an additional nine cents in national currency for every dollar of tax, and the second installment will include an additional three cents and seven li (a subunit of currency) in national currency for every dollar of tax. Taxpayers must pay the first installment in full within three months and the second installment within two months from the start of collection. The start dates for the two installments are divided into three categories: Category A: April 1st for the first installment and October 1st for the second installment. Category B: May 1st for the first installment and November 1st for the second installment. Category C: June 1st for the first installment and December 1st for the second installment. Instructions have been issued to all districts, townships, and towns to comply. 82

Anqing Bribery Case Transferred to Court for Trial. The Anqing Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association's case involving the unsealing of Japanese goods and bribery for personal gain is being actively pursued by the Provincial Party Rectification Committee for disposition. At the 83rd regular meeting of the Provincial Rectification Committee on the 23rd, Qiu Jizu reported on the interrogation of Wu Tianfeng and others. It was unanimously decided to disband the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, appoint new personnel to reorganize it, and remove Zhang Congzhou, the instructor sent by the Provincial Rectification Committee to the association. All case files related to bribery and profit-sharing have been transferred to the court for strict investigation and trial. However, key figures involved, including instructor Zhang Congzhou and committee members Su Xiaodong, Ding Rongtong, Ma Fengsheng, Chen Honghai, Tan Hongzhi, Pan Zhongshun, and Lang Yongming, have all fled to avoid punishment and have not been apprehended. The Provincial Rectification Committee yesterday transferred the entire case file to the Huaining District Court for legal proceedings. 83

Financial Difficulties of Anhui's Education Funding. Anhui Province's education funding relies on a monthly central government subsidy of 100,000 yuan, which is almost entirely depended upon for the regular expenses of schools throughout the province. After the start of the second half of last year, the Finance Department only disbursed two and a half months' worth of subsidies, covering August, September, and half of October. As of the end of December, the Finance Department owed a total of 250,000 yuan, plus the previous debt of 195,000 yuan, totaling 445,000 yuan. The Anhui Education Department has tried its best to maintain operations, but the provincial treasury is also strained due to the impact of floods. It managed to scrape together enough to pay about two months and 80% of the regular expenses for various schools in the second half of last year, which was already extremely difficult and involved a great deal of effort. Although the schools are currently on break, they are unable to close accounts properly. Salaries and office expenses are almost three months in arrears. The need for funds is urgent. The provincial government has repeatedly telegraphed the Finance Department on the 7th and 11th of this month, urging the allocation of funds, stating that the salaries of teachers and staff in Anhui's schools are several months in arrears, making it impossible to close out the semester. The next semester is about to begin, and it will be difficult to start without settling the arrears. The survival of education is in great danger. We implore the Finance Department to consider the difficult situation of education in Anhui Province and find a special way to allocate the 445,000 yuan in arrears to provide relief. Furthermore, Cheng Bin, the head of the province's education funding management office, has been in Beijing for several days, seeking immediate allocation of the arrears and discussing long-term plans for stabilizing and ensuring Anhui's education funding. It is also reported that representatives from various schools in the province have gone to the Finance Department to petition for all education funding issues. Since Yang Zhongming took over as the acting director of the provincial education department, his familiarity with Anhui's education sector has allowed him to streamline operations and improve efficiency. His ability to maintain stability during this time of severe financial constraints is truly remarkable. It is now learned that Yang has repeatedly telegraphed the new director, He Qigong, urging him to come to Anhui to take over, so that he can be relieved of his duties, as the schools are currently on break and require numerous matters to be handled. 86

Yu Qingtang Visits Bengbu to Inspect the Establishment of Public Education Groups in the Industrial Revitalization Zone. Yu Qingtang, the third section chief of the Jiangsu Education Department, recognizing that many workers in the disaster areas of northern Anhui are uneducated laborers, specifically consulted with the Northern Anhui 12th District Industrial Revitalization Bureau to implement appropriate education for the disaster-affected workers. He especially instructed various social education institutions in Jiangsu to organize public education groups in the Industrial Revitalization Zone. Out of caution, Yu personally came to conduct on-site inspections. On the 21st, he arrived in Bengbu with Tang Moubo and Zhao Guangtao. On the morning of the 22nd, he crossed the Huai River to investigate and express his condolences in various disaster relief work villages. That evening, he visited educational institutions, with a particular focus on social education facilities. Yu will return to Zhenjiang on the 22nd and pass through Nanjing, where he will finalize the organization of the group and begin work in Bengbu soon. 87

Huang Shiheng Firmly Declines the Presidency of Hunan University. Hunan University is the highest institution of learning in Hunan Province. The position of president was originally held by Cao Dianqiu, who has now taken office as the Director of the Hunan Education Department and cannot handle both roles. The provincial government then appointed Huang Wangheng, the previous Director of the Education Department, as his successor. However, Huang firmly declined and suggested that the provincial government abolish the position of president and instead establish a committee, with the deans of the university's three colleges (Arts, Science, and Engineering) serving as standing committee members to oversee university affairs. However, the committee system was deemed to lack accountability, and Huang was urged to take office as soon as possible. Huang remains resolute in his refusal and has also stated that if the system is changed to a committee, he would only be willing to serve as an ordinary committee member. His appointment has been returned. 88

Emergency Representative Meeting of University Student Unions in This City Passes 14 Important Resolutions After Attendance of 50 Representatives from 20 Schools. Representatives from Fudan and other schools expressed condolences to the striking workers at the Japanese factory. Since the entire workforce of over 5,000 Chinese workers at the Japanese-owned Towa Cotton Mill in this city went on strike on the 12th of this month due to the factory's dismissal of over 130 workers and the cancellation of monthly bonuses, for half a month, over 60,000 striking Chinese workers have been suffering from hunger and cold, and their pain is indescribable. Recognizing this and feeling their patriotic enthusiasm and unwavering determination, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of Universities in this city appointed Wan Ziwei from Fudan University, Lai Yihou from Zhonggong, and Chen Haoru from Dongya to express condolences and investigate the suffering and circumstances of the past ten days or so, in order to engage in fundraising and assistance. The strike committee answered each question in detail and stated that they would not resume work unless the factory sincerely responds to the 13 demands. 89

Free Talk: "Not Removing the Court Grass" (Zhai Fu's Discussion)

The Qualifications of a County Magistrate (Continued)

So, should county magistrates not have qualifications and not need to take exams? The county magistrates of tomorrow must be examined while in office. Their political achievements will be their solid qualifications. Each incumbent county magistrate must submit a paper: "How much benefit has been brought to the people of this county, and how much corruption has been eliminated?" To break it down: Every county magistrate must complete the following tasks to pass:

(1) How many schools have been opened since taking office, how many students have been added, and how many scientific children, scientific youths, and scientific adults have been cultivated?

(2) How many miles of roads have been built since taking office?

(3) How many trees have been planted since taking office?

(4) How many water conservancy projects have been built since taking office?

(5) How many new agricultural and industrial production methods have been promoted since taking office

National Government Relief Committee Fund Revenue and Expenditure Audit Report by the Financial and Accounting Groups

General Overview of Revenue and Expenditure: Since the start of relief efforts on September 10th of last year, they have been dependent on financial resources. After the establishment of the National Government Flood Relief Committee, a financial group was established to manage the treasury, fundraising, purchasing, and international transportation. However, the disaster area was vast, the disaster was severe, and the government's finances were strained, making fundraising difficult. An agreement was made to borrow American wheat, which did not require immediate payment, but the urgent need for post-disaster relief could not be delayed. Since its establishment, the Financial Group has spared no effort in soliciting donations from domestic and foreign individuals and organizations, and has received enthusiastic support from all walks of life, with remarkable results. The receipt of relief funds since April has been announced and acknowledged on a weekly basis. The revenue and expenditure situation is analyzed and described as follows:

Analysis of Revenue and Expenditure Items: Up to the end of December 20, the Financial Group received a total of: National currency: $7,798,092.88; US dollars: $471,264.67.

National currency items include donations from all sectors at home and abroad: $6,875,456.05; US dollar allocations: $624,053.76 (equivalent to US$150,000); funds entrusted by the Flood Relief Associations of various provinces to make cotton clothes: $162,000; funds transferred from Fuxin Flour Company for American wheat: $131,383.36; returned surplus funds from Jiangxi rice procurement: $5,150; bank interest: $49.71.

US dollar items: US$471,264.67, is the loan of £140,000 from HSBC by the National Government Relief Committee, using customs duties and disaster relief surcharges to pay for American wheat transportation. The annual interest rate is 7%. Because customs duties are calculated in gold units, the loan is also converted into US dollars and deposited in the Central Bank.

Based on the payment certificates approved by the audit group, the expenditures of the Financial Group up to the end of last December amounted to a total of: National currency: $7,484,545.59; US dollars: $422,742.24.

Expenditures include: Allocations to the disaster area work groups for emergency relief in various provinces: $3,600,138.72 (including US$457,144.35 donated by the American Red Cross for relief in Hubei); $50,000 for the Capital Reception Center; $20,000 for the Shanghai Reception Center; $215,000 for emergency engineering fees and construction fees in the industrial relief area; $131,585 for emergency relief investigation and distribution expenses in various regions; and a total of $45,115.96 for aircraft surveying fees, relief inspection work, and inspector travel expenses.

Expenditures handled by the Financial Group totaled $1,700,758.87, including over $1,165,000 for cotton clothing and bedding, over $379,000 for flour, and $300,000 disbursed by the Health and Epidemic Prevention Group for medicines and expenses. The cost of American wheat was also substantial, with over $553,000 spent on transportation alone, and over US$300,000. The loan from HSBC by the former National Government Relief Committee was used to cover the transportation costs of American wheat. Other expenses, such as the cost of wheat sacks, amounted to over $316,000, and the water transportation expenses for various grain stations amounted to over $137,000.

The above are the major expenditure items. After offsetting revenue and expenditure, there is still a surplus of $313,547.29 in national currency and US$48,522.43.

Decline in Relief Fund Income: From August 19 to December 31, 20, the Financial Group received a total of $6,875,456.05 in relief funds, which has been announced on a weekly basis. In the early stages of the flood, people from all walks of life generously donated to support relief efforts. From September 1st to 10th, the average daily income of relief funds was over $150,000; from September 11th to 20th, the average daily income was over $110,000. Since then, it has been declining. In the most recent period, from January 11th to 20th, the average daily income was only over $3,300, of which donations from overseas Chinese accounted for about 60%. At a time when all industries across the country are declining, the ability of the Chinese people to assist in relief efforts is limited. However, the achievements are commendable. Since the invasion by the Japanese army, the whole country has been in turmoil, and the Chinese people are urgently seeking foreign aid. Internal disasters have gradually been forgotten, which is a major disaster for the 50 million victims.

Difficulties in Fundraising for Relief Efforts: The difficulty of disaster relief is not in the initial emergency relief, but in the implementation of post-disaster plans and fundraising. It has been five months since the flood occurred. Subsequent relief work will focus on the implementation of industrial and agricultural relief. The embankments that collapsed in various provinces will be repaired by the National Government Relief Committee. This project is enormous. American wheat can only cover wages. All other expenses require cash. The losses suffered by farmers in this flood are extremely serious. According to a survey by the Department of Agricultural Economics of Nanjing Jinling University, the losses of farmers in the Jianghuai River basin are estimated at $200 million. The urgent needs of the victims are over $150 million. With spring plowing approaching, post-disaster measures such as embankment repair and seed loans are urgent. American wheat has ended its continuous shipment to China. The transportation cost is substantial and must be paid on time to avoid delaying relief efforts. The above items are all necessary. Industrial and agricultural relief work and American wheat transportation are interconnected and cannot be separated in terms of urgency. Regarding the source of relief funds, the recent daily average income of donations from all sectors is only over $3,000, which is expected to continue to decline. The $30 million disaster relief bonds resolved by the former National Government have not been issued to date. Customs surcharge revenue, as of the end of last December, was only $900,000. Railway passenger ticket surcharges have not been reported by various railway bureaus. In total, as of the end of December, the National Government Flood Relief Committee's expenditure shortfall was approximately $2 million. The £140,000 borrowed from HSBC earlier was used to cover this shortfall. After January, customs surcharge revenue will be allocated to HSBC on a monthly basis to repay the loan in full. The Financial Group has consulted with the Public Debt Fund Management Committee to allocate funds from the $30 million disaster relief bonds that were approved by the former National Government but not issued, to maintain relief efforts. It is estimated that $1.5 million can be allocated in January and $1.7 million can be allocated in February. After March, as American wheat transportation costs decrease, all expenses are expected to be covered by customs surcharge revenue.

An Interesting Case Involving Monk Zhiwen: Arrested for Opium Use, Police Take Photos, Marriage Certificate, and Another Document of Separation

Long-Haired, Robed, Scarred Monk with a Wife and Illegitimate Daughter. Jing'an Temple in West Shanghai is a famous ancient temple that is known for its incense. Recently, Zhiwen, also known as Xu Jinsheng, a monk from the temple, was found to be consuming opium and married to a local woman, Li Cuiyun (27 years old), with whom he has a two-year-old daughter. They lived together in the back room of No. 9 Dahua Lane on Bair Road in the French Concession. The abbot of the temple and donor Wang Banjiang (a teacher at Jing'an Elementary School) found out about this. They believed that the monk's behavior violated the precepts and damaged the temple's reputation. Therefore, Wang, representing the temple, reported to the French Concession Police Station at 8:00 AM the day before yesterday. The head of the police sent detectives Hang Guangfu and Jin Chengshan to arrest him at the address. When they arrived, they found opium paraphernalia in the room. Zhiwen was at home and was immediately arrested. The police took photos of the scene and found a marriage certificate for Li Cuiyun, dated April 3, 13th year of the Republic. It stated: Marriage Certificate: Xu Jinsheng (Zhiwen) and Li Cuiyun. Witness: Min Heng. Matchmaker: Xu Gengsheng and Li Qiaoyun. Master of Ceremony: Li Wenkui. The invitation card read: "A Hundred Years of Harmony." There was also a document of separation between Qian Xiuying and Xu Jinsheng, stating that she received 2,000 silver dollars and would forever sever relations with Xu Jinsheng. It was dated August of the 20th year of the Republic and certified by lawyer Chen Zemin. The detectives brought everything to the police station and sent them to the Second Special Court yesterday. Zhiwen wore a gray crepe de chine camel robe, a silk satin jacket, and a Russian hat. His hair was short, and when he took off his hat, the scars from his ordination were clearly visible. At 3:00 PM, Judge Zhang Shijie, together with Prosecutor Lou Guanguang, took the bench in the Fourth Court to interrogate him. First, police lawyer Gu Shouxi presented the case, stating that the police received a report that the defendant was consuming opium. When they went to arrest him, they found opium paraphernalia in the room, so they took photos, arrested the defendant, and sent him to court for prosecution according to the anti-opium law. He requested a postponement to allow the police to investigate. The plaintiff, Wang Banjiang, also recounted the events. When questioned, Zhiwen admitted that his name was Xu Jinsheng but denied consuming opium. Li Cuiyun, holding her child, testified that when the defendant married her, he said he worked at the stock exchange. At that time, he had long hair, and she did not see the scars, so she did not know he was a monk. Judge Zhang ordered a postponement for further questioning and ordered the defendant to be returned to the police station.

Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant to Expand

According to Huadong News Agency, the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Department is expanding. According to the director of the department, Zeng Yijing, the construction of new buildings has already begun and is scheduled to be completed by the end of June. Behind the existing factory buildings, a new aircraft assembly plant will be built, 121 feet deep and 50 feet wide, capable of housing six aircraft. On both sides, there will be two-story buildings, 23 feet wide, with the upper floor serving as office space and the lower floor as factories. The entire structure will be steel-framed, with a total construction cost of over 200,000 yuan. This year, it has been decided to manufacture six new aircraft. Construction has already begun. Each aircraft will have 220 horsepower. The first aircraft is scheduled to be completed in July, the second in August, the third in September, the fourth in October, the fifth in November, and the sixth in December. The design will be the same as the newly completed Jiangfeng and Jianghe aircraft. At the same time, a 400-horsepower fighter plane will be manufactured on a trial basis. If the test is successful, mass production can begin next year. Two Moths-type aircraft, rebuilt by the department, have been completed. One has been completed, and the other will be completed by the end of this month. Each aircraft has 90 horsepower and has been named Jiangjiu and Jiang _. They are both training aircraft. In addition, the department plans to gradually establish its own engine manufacturing plant and add machinery to transform manual manufacturing into mechanical manufacturing to accelerate production. If funding is available, this can be carried out. Given China's current situation, aircraft are the most suitable for national defense.

Ministry of Finance Responds to Correct Two Types of Taxes

Shanghai Special District Citizens Federation previously sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance requesting the correction of the stamp tax penalty rules and the license tax stamp procedures. Yesterday, the Ministry of Finance replied with Yin Zi No. 97, stating: "We have received the telegram. The current stamp tax penalty rules, ranging from a minimum of 5 yuan to a maximum of 100 yuan, are already much lighter than the revised tax law of the 3rd year of the Republic, which had penalties up to 200 yuan. These rules are stipulated by regulations and have been implemented for a long time, making it difficult to arbitrarily change them. There are also explicit provisions for stamp duties to be affixed to tobacco and alcohol licenses, and various provinces have been following them for years. It is difficult for the province to be unique. However, for the sake of factual convenience, the stamping procedures for these licenses should be approved by the tobacco and alcohol licensing agencies to follow the tax rates set by the Ministry when filling out the forms and affixing stamps, and merchants should pay the ticket price in full when obtaining the licenses to simplify the process. We have ordered the Jiangsu Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau to order its subordinates to comply."

Request to the National Government to Dismiss Chen and Support Zhang

Telegram from the Anhui Provincial People's Self-Rescue Federation to the National Government

To Chairman Lin of the National Government, President Sun of the Executive Yuan, and Members of the Standing Committee of the Central Political Conference:

Chen Diaoyuan, Chairman of Anhui Province, has committed numerous crimes of harming the country and the people, violating laws and disrupting order. The people of Anhui, both inside and outside the province, have urgently appealed against him repeatedly. The National Government's Supervisory Yuan has filed a well-founded impeachment for corruption, which need not be detailed. This time, the central government is rebuilding and determined to reform domestic affairs. The first priority is to eliminate the scourge of warlords and relieve the people's suffering. People like Chen Diaoyuan have no place in a country that is vigorously implementing democratic politics. The people of Anhui are in imminent danger, and relief cannot be delayed even for a day. There are many ways to liberate the people, but the most urgent task is to build a clean and honest government and have a well-disciplined anti-bandit army that strictly enforces the law, so that corruption dare not run rampant in the countryside and order is gradually restored. Shao Yun and others are either farmers or engaged in industry and commerce and have never been involved in politics. However, because of the personal interests and the deep feelings we have, we only know that Mr. Zhang Zhijiang, the current Director of Pacification of Jiangsu, has the spirit of hard work and endurance of the Northwest Army and always cares about the people's livelihood. Although he does not hold military power, his former subordinates, such as Liang Guanying, Zhang Huatang, and Zheng Tingzhen, are full of morale and strict discipline and are happy to listen to Zhang's command. During his year in Jiangsu, he not only achieved remarkable results in suppressing bandits, but also won the deep love and respect of the people. Last year, when there was a major flood, he was able to use his spare time to supervise soldiers to help the people reinforce the dikes in advance and organize emergency relief afterwards. Other efforts to benefit the people are too numerous to mention. Since Jiangsu and Anhui are geographically close, the people of Anhui feel how fortunate the people of Jiangsu are and how miserable the people of Anhui are. We humbly believe that you are concerned about the suffering of the people and are eager to quickly eliminate the scourge of Chen for the people of Anhui and to find a successor who can save Anhui. We dare to uphold the central government's principle of adopting public opinion and represent the public opinion of 300,000 people in Anhui, believing that the person who is not an active soldier but has the power to command, is extremely diligent and honest in his work, and is able to empathize with the people's suffering is Mr. Zhang Zhijiang, the Director of Pacification, who can remedy the damage caused by Chen Diaoyuan and is the resurrection medicine for the people of Anhui. The people of Anhui are eagerly awaiting this and can also convince Chen Diaoyuan and prevent him from making excuses. Shao Yun and others are from the countryside and have no personal grievances. We only want peace in our homeland and the restoration of our old careers. We are different from bureaucrats and politicians who use politics to seek activity. Our sincerity is clear to the world. We humbly request you to examine and approve our request and implement it quickly. We are extremely grateful and devoted.

Representatives of the Anhui Provincial People's Self-Rescue Federation: Tian Shaoyun, Tian Weilin, Ma Chengzhi, Liu Changshi, Xiang Guangfu, Zhang Yizhai, Tian Minxian, Zhou Yuanyu, Wang Zaitian, Lei Zhendong, Tang Mingda, Liu Zhenguo, Sun Yuzhu, Li Dingbang, Zhu Yongnian, Sheng Fuxue, and others, 3,650 people in total.

The National Lawyers Association of the Republic of China sent a letter to the Lawyers Associations of various provinces yesterday, stating: "We are writing to inform you that the Executive and Supervisory Committee of the Association held a meeting on the 17th of this month. The special donation should be paid to the Association in two weeks for distant provinces and one week for nearby provinces. We are notifying your Association for your information and request that you pay the special donation in accordance with the resolution to maintain the Association's operations. Yours truly."

Notice of Factory Registration

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Association sent a letter to the factory workers of the various associations yesterday, stating: "We are writing to inform you that we have received an instruction from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, which states: 'We have received an order from the Municipal Government approving the consultation from the Ministry of Industry regarding the registration of factories. As the industrial records of our country are lacking in detail, it is inconvenient for industrial administration. The Ministry has formulated twelve articles of factory registration rules and two types of appendices and submitted them to the Executive Yuan for approval and filing. They were promulgated and implemented by the Ministry on the 18th of this month. In addition to sending the rules and appendices to the provincial and municipal governments for implementation, we are also sending a set of the rules and appendices to your Municipal Government for your information and request that the competent bureau follow the regulations and announce them and present them for filing within a time limit. In the future, those factories that apply for awards according to various incentive regulations should be asked to apply for registration first and then forwarded for review.' In accordance with this, we are copying a set of the rules and appendices and ordering your bureau to comply and also issuing a copy of the rules and appendices for your Association to comply with and inform the various factories. We are enclosing two types of factory registration rules and registration appendices for your information."

News about the Construction of Civilian Housing in Pudong

Reply from the Municipal Government to the Municipal Party Department

The Municipal Government sent a letter to the Municipal Party Department yesterday regarding the construction of civilian housing in Pudong, stating: "We are writing to inform you that the Bureau of Social Affairs has reported the following: 'We are reporting in reply to the Municipal Government's Instruction No. 27, which states: We have examined the documents in the file and approved the letter from the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipal Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang, stating that the Fifth District Party Department has requested to build civilian housing in Pudong to benefit the shed households and enhance the city's appearance. The Standing Committee has resolved to request your review and reply. We are enclosing the original and duplicate documents for your examination and request that the relevant bureaus discuss and reply. With this order, the attachments are returned.' In accordance with this, the funds available for the construction of civilian housing this year include 120,000 yuan in temporary expenses approved by your government and included in the 20th year general budget, plus over 178,400 yuan in surplus funds borrowed from the Municipal Bank last year, which can be used to build about 800 or 900 houses. In order to save management costs, meet the needs of shed households, and improve the city's appearance, the Bureau of Public Works, Public Security, Finance, and Social Affairs have agreed to add 200 houses to the First Civilian Housing and 700 houses near the Third Housing and submitted their opinions to your government for approval on September 23, 20th year and received Instruction No. 121234 on October 13, stating: 'We have reviewed the report and learned that the case has been approved by the 192nd Municipal Meeting to add 200 houses near the First Civilian Housing and 300 houses near the Third Civilian Housing and to consider adding more houses near Tanzawan or other suitable locations within the scope of the designated funds. We are ordering you to comply.' In accordance with this, the Bureau of Public Works convened the relevant bureaus on January 4th of this year to discuss the location of the new housing. In addition to expanding the First Civilian Housing and temporarily suspending the addition of new houses to the Third Civilian Housing, it was decided to lease the Jinghu Railway base to build the Fourth Housing. The location is west of Datong Road, south of the railway, and north of Jinling Road. The ground is flat and the rent is cheaper, which is more suitable than renting private land. The Land Bureau has sent personnel to contact the leasing. In accordance with the order to review the reasons for building civilian housing in Pudong, we propose to wait for the completion of the survey and measurement of the location and then make a further decision. If there is no balance, the funds will be limited by the budget, and we can only wait for the next year to add more houses. In accordance with the previous order, we have consulted with the relevant bureaus and have reached a consensus. We are submitting the original report and requesting your review and approval. We are respectfully submitting the original and duplicate reports.' In accordance with this, in addition to ordering the release of the instruction and printing it, we are sending a letter to your committee for your information. The original report is attached." (Remainder of the letter omitted)

Details of the Robbery at the Dawang Temple

The home of Tao Yongsheng, a resident of No. 87 Dawang Temple Street, Nanshi, was robbed yesterday around noon. His daughter, Deshu, attempted to call the police and jumped from the drying platform, injuring herself. The details are recorded below:

Yongsheng's Situation: Tao Yongsheng, 45 years old, from Zhenjiang, has been working as a Chinese language teacher at Shanghai Middle School and Dadongmen Yucai Middle School. His wife, Xu, 33 years old, has three daughters: the eldest, Dezhen, 21 years old; the second, Deshu, 19 years old; and the youngest, Defen, 17 years old. They are all studying at Qingxin Girls' Middle School in Chenjiabang. Tao's monthly income is quite good, so the family lives comfortably.

Sudden Arrival of Three Robbers: Yesterday around noon, Tao was out and had not returned home. The family was having lunch in the living room when they suddenly heard a loud noise of someone breaking the door at the back. The maid opened the back door, and three men entered: one wearing a yellow coat and two wearing blue cloth short shirts and pants, speaking in the local dialect. They entered the living room and showed a handgun to intimidate them into silence. Tao's wife and daughters realized they were being robbed and were terrified. The robbers immediately went upstairs and ransacked the bedroom, overturning boxes and cabinets. They took a Shanghai Bank passbook, five silver dollars, and two gold rings from the box and fled with the stolen goods.

When the Police Arrived: Tao's neighbors noticed what was happening and immediately went to report to the police. However, the location was far from the post. When Yang Shilong, the guard from the 24th post, heard the alarm and rushed to the scene, the robbers had already fled with the stolen goods from the front door. The police immediately gave chase. The robbers realized that the police were chasing them and hastily pulled out a gun and fired a shot behind them. Fortunately, it missed. The police continued to chase bravely without firing a shot. However, there were many small alleys in the area, so the robbers quickly disappeared from sight and could not be caught.

Deshu Injured: During the robbery, Tao's second daughter, Deshu, took the opportunity to sneak onto the drying platform and jumped down to call the police. However, she lost her footing and fell to the ground, injuring her waist. Her condition was very serious. Tao's family sent her to the hospital for treatment.

Record of the Retrial of Murderer Yan Jinbiao: Yan's Mother Testifies in Court

Was Li Guocheng the Killer?

On the afternoon of August 15th of last year, at 6:00 PM, a robbery and murder occurred in Room 2 of the Fashang Inn on Xixinqiao Street in the French Concession. Jiang Zhonghan, Xia Yongsheng, and a man surnamed Xue were killed, and Zhong Ziqing was injured. The police arrested the suspect, Yan Jinbiao, from Funing, and sent him to the Second Special Court. According to his confession, Li Guocheng was the mastermind. Yan was sentenced to death. Yan appealed, but the High Third Branch upheld the death sentence. Yan then appealed to the Supreme Court. Li Guocheng, the main criminal in this case, was arrested by the Public Security Bureau in the Chinese Concession at the end of last year. Yan filed a petition with the court to cross-examine him. The court transferred Li to the case and sent him to the police station of the French Concession for investigation. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Tribunal of the Second Special Court. The criminal court president, Ge Zhiqin, together with Prosecutor Lou Guanguang, took the bench to interrogate him. Li stated that he was 33 years old, from Funing, also known as Li Dongliang, and adopted the surname Chen, so he was also known as Chen Youliang. He lived in Goucun, Funing. The judge ordered the case to be retried. First, police lawyer Gu Shouxi presented the case, prosecuting him for murder according to the criminal law. First, Yan's mother, Yan Liangshi, stated that Jinbiao was her second son. Her eldest son had died, and her youngest son was at home. Her daughter-in-law told her that Li Guocheng was the killer. Her daughter-in-law was not present because she was not feeling well. Xu Jiangshi stated that Jiang Zhonghan was her elder brother. He told her that he had a feud with Li Guocheng. Later, she read in the newspaper that he was beaten to death by Li, so she filed a petition to seek justice. Her sister-in-law had returned to her home in Jiangbei. At this point, the judge ordered Yan Jinbiao to be brought to court. Yan stated that he did not call Jiang and the other three to the inn. On June 28th of the lunar calendar, Li Guocheng, Yang Jiucheng, Liu Wu, and Zhang San discussed killing someone at his house. On July 1st, Li and the other three invited Jiang Zhonghan to his house, treated him to tea, and gave him two silver dollars, asking Jiang to invite Xia and the others to the inn. At 5:00 PM on the 2nd, Li and the other three came to his house again. They first ordered noodles and ate until 7:00 PM. Li Guocheng and Yang Jiucheng went to beat them, and Liu Wu and Zhang San went to keep watch. Before leaving, they told him to stay at home and said that if they did not see him at home when they returned, they would kill him. So he waited at home. Later, Yang Jiucheng came and said that one person was not killed and recognized them, telling him to leave quickly. That night, he spent the night on the street. The next morning, he asked his cousin Dai Yunhong to visit his house and was arrested by detectives. Dai then led the detectives to Tiancheng Lane and arrested him. He was truly wronged and asked the judge to ask Li Guocheng to tell the truth. Was he present at the time and did he discuss going to shoot and kill? The previous confession was due to unbearable torture. As for the robbery, Shi Chengwen and others in the prison told him to admit to it. He asked for them to be brought in for questioning. When questioned, Li Guocheng flatly denied the murder. At that time, he was at the Public Security Bureau in Goucun in his hometown. He asked for an investigation. Yan Jinbiao had previously been a thief in Jiangbei and was driven away by him, so he falsely accused him out of hatred. He asked for clarification and hired a lawyer to defend him. At this point, Yan's mother stated again that Li Guocheng was the killer and had promised to give her daughter-in-law 2,000 silver dollars. She asked for a clear verdict. Judge Ge reviewed the statements and ordered a postponement for further questioning on February 9th. Li Guocheng was returned to custody.
